  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8527e1fc-23e3-46e4-b39c-e7f9d8cae9b2'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

It gives you more on the story line of each book if you read them in order.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1646128245" class="readable"

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4523198300956192167"><b> 1 FAILED ALPHA STAR </b><br/><br/>I hated this book so much!<br/>I can't even say anything nice about it. <br/><br/><b>SPOILERS AHEAD READ AND BE WARNED! </b><br/><br/>Disclaimer: my opinion is of the unpopular variety.<br/><br/>First off the heroine Lily is forced to raises her baby girl alone while he stands by the bitch slut he knowingly had sex right before the heroine.<br/>Like gross or what! Then he breaks up with her over text after he took her virginity. <br/>So you may ask yourself what does she do when she see him at the park some years later? After</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer880366422" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10722623604142791259">I don't even know where to start. There are SO many things I didn't like about this book. I'm afraid if I point them out I'll never finish this review. <br/><br/>Okay, how about if we start off with the fact that Cash breaks up with Lily a day after he took her virginity. No explanations, no excuses, straight to the point, "we're done, bye." <br/>Ouch. So much for her being 'the one'<br/><br/>Then, Lily finds out she's pregnant. The fact that she's 19 and has no car, money, and is living off a scholarship, AND doesn't f</span>
  <span id="freeText10722623604142791259" style="display:none">I don't even know where to start. There are SO many things I didn't like about this book. I'm afraid if I point them out I'll never finish this review. <br /><br />Okay, how about if we start off with the fact that Cash breaks up with Lily a day after he took her virginity. No explanations, no excuses, straight to the point, "we're done, bye." <br />Ouch. So much for her being 'the one'<br /><br />Then, Lily finds out she's pregnant. The fact that she's 19 and has no car, money, and is living off a scholarship, AND doesn't freak out that she's going to be a single mom? Give me a break. <br />Having a baby is a huge deal especially if you're doing it on your own. She takes it so cooly as if she just found out she needs to take an extra class. <br /><br />Add four years later, Lily is in the park with her daughter and sees Cash with Jax (his son) and automatically Cash knows Ashlyn is his daughter. This little girl must look identical to Cash ( who knows, the author gives so little details.) Anyway, again, Lilly takes it so cooly to see him. <br />Am I the only one who was angry that she doesn't do anything? The dude texted you saying to abort your baby? (Yeah yeah later on he says he didn't do it but whatever) <br /><br />Then, Cash fresh as a lettuce, decides its time to take Lily back again. God, the nerve this guy. So Lily is an object you can drop and pick up whenever the hell you want? <br />Someone shoot me. <br />Here's what pisses me off the most. Lily is a freaking doormat that takes it all. He wanted her back and she's okay with it. He says he loves her and she says back. <br /><br />This is where I stopped-- when they got back together. About the seven or eight chapter. I can't stand that she's too passive and she never pushes back.<br /><br />It just wasn't my cup of tea, onto something better. <br /></span>

<div id="review_770167885" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/770167885" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/770167885?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer770167885" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11174301157019804174"><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/54c43d49-942f-4a69-97c2-154b48a3d8b4_zpsad246245.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809191.jpg' alt=' photo 54c43d49-942f-4a69-97c2-154b48a3d8b4_zpsad246245.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’ve really enjoyed reading the ‘Until’ series. Both <i>Until November</i> and <i>Until Trevor</i> were fantastic books. I am very happy to say that <i>Until Lilly</i> was even better! For sure my favorite in the series (so far!)<br/><br/>Cash and Lilly have history. When they met, they fell hard. Cash knew right away that Lilly was the one for him. Unfortunately, life got in the way. Cash was left to make an impossible decision and the choice he made took Lilly away from him. It also gave him his son, Jaxon who h</span>
  <span id="freeText11174301157019804174" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/54c43d49-942f-4a69-97c2-154b48a3d8b4_zpsad246245.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809191.jpg" alt=" photo 54c43d49-942f-4a69-97c2-154b48a3d8b4_zpsad246245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’ve really enjoyed reading the ‘Until’ series. Both <i>Until November</i> and <i>Until Trevor</i> were fantastic books. I am very happy to say that <i>Until Lilly</i> was even better! For sure my favorite in the series (so far!)<br><br>Cash and Lilly have history. When they met, they fell hard. Cash knew right away that Lilly was the one for him. Unfortunately, life got in the way. Cash was left to make an impossible decision and the choice he made took Lilly away from him. It also gave him his son, Jaxon who he loves more than life. He is away from his crazy ex, has custody of his son, life is good. Or as good as it can be without Lilly. <br><br>After Cash left Lilly, she was devastated. Then, she found out she was pregnant. With Cash’s baby. Due to a certain someone, Lilly was left pregnant, alone, and finishing school as a single mother. Her life isn’t perfect, but she wouldn’t trade her daughter for the world. She’s never ‘gotten over’ Cash, but she’s gotten used to being alone. <br><br>When Cash see’s Lilly with a little girl that looks identical to his son, he is shocked. When he finds out what happened all those years ago, he’s going to do whatever it takes. He’s has to win Lilly back and get his family together. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/8e010b6d-452e-4247-82c4-22979e8a85a2_zpsde12ee7b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809192.jpg" alt=" photo 8e010b6d-452e-4247-82c4-22979e8a85a2_zpsde12ee7b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>Lilly is someone who I will never take for granted, because I know how it feels to be without her and the light that she brings to my life.</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Cash is determined to make Lilly his. She was his once, she loved him once, he knows he can get her to fall for him again. Lilly doesn’t want to go there with Cash. She’s afraid. He broke her once, she’s not sure if she can go through that kind of heart ache again. She wants her daughter to know her father and brother, so she spends a lot of time with Cash. She wants to hate him, but she can’t. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why can’t I hate you?” Her words are quiet, and I can hardly make them out.<br>I whisper into her ear before kissing her under it, “Because I am your one, too.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/88589fe1-1c51-49ac-a39a-9c573c12baf3_zps84905061.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809193.jpg" alt=" photo 88589fe1-1c51-49ac-a39a-9c573c12baf3_zps84905061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The more time Lilly and Cash spend together as a family, the more Lilly see’s how great it really could be for the four of them. It’s not even a matter of falling back into love with Cash. How could it be? She never stopped loving him to begin with. He wants to build something with her. Something real and true. How can she resist... <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I know we have a lot to work on, and I know that it’s going to take time for us to rebuild what was broken, but I also know that if we do, we will have something that is beyond anything that either of us thought possible.”</blockquote>
</i><br>What is it about those Mayson brothers??? Ah! I love them all! Cash Mayson is a special kind of guy. He’s a devoted father, loving, kind, but also possessive, dominant and that wonderful alpha male we all love. Did I mention he was super duper hot and sexy... because he is!<br><i>
  <blockquote>"You have the perfect ass babe."<br>"What?" I breathe, feeling goose bumps form across my skin.<br>"I can't wait to get my hands on it and turn it red, so please, try to piss me off. It will just get me what I want faster." </blockquote>
</i><br>Then there is Lilly. 100% my favorite heroine of the series so far. Her strength, loving and forgiving nature, and the way she was with Jax. It made me love her that much more. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/286df4fe-ca34-451d-bc58-4ceecd12c489_zpsf5010a32.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809194.jpg" alt=" photo 286df4fe-ca34-451d-bc58-4ceecd12c489_zpsf5010a32.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am a sucker for second chance romances. This wasn’t your typical story line, which I liked. There are more elements at play. The kids made me laugh and smile. Cash made me swoon. I was engaged from start to finish. <br>The only thing I didn’t love was that damn ex of Cash’s. She infuriated me. An entire new breed of crazy. Was there maybe a little excessive/over the top drama from the bat shit crazy ex? Yes. Was it enough to take away from my 5 star rating? Hell no! <br><br>I say this is my favorite in the series so far, because I am very intrigued by the tattooed bad boy Nico Mayson...<br><i>“I found my boom. I had no fucking clue that returning a lost phone would lead me to her, but I fucking found her.”</i> <br>After reading the sneak peek to Nico’s book- I’m excited!!!<br><br><br>A second chance at your first love, family, loyalty, high on the steam and thoroughly entertaining. This book was a winner for me. A highly recommend book from a highly recommend series! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%204/1c649ae9-9f88-4bff-8aec-83a7854504b8_zpsc1c733e8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394109231i/8809195.jpg" alt=" photo 1c649ae9-9f88-4bff-8aec-83a7854504b8_zpsc1c733e8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=steamy-romance">steamy-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer865395324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15223739650847767408"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393621563i/8741315._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I'm going to make you fall in love with me again.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434595ra/877296.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Now I have a confession to make here.<br/><b>*whispers*</b><i> I didn't like book 1. </i><br/>*Ducks for flying tomatoes*<br/>Now now, don't get all judgy with me here. I loved the set up and idea behind the book. I just wasn't big on the delivery. As in, the heroine drove me slightly batty. The 2nd book was better, but there was still something missing for me.<br/><br/>Now you're probably sitting there and thinking to yourself, why is this crazy bitch reading book</span>
  <span id="freeText15223739650847767408" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393621563i/8741315._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I'm going to make you fall in love with me again.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434595ra/877296.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now I have a confession to make here.<br><b>*whispers*</b><i> I didn't like book 1. </i><br>*Ducks for flying tomatoes*<br>Now now, don't get all judgy with me here. I loved the set up and idea behind the book. I just wasn't big on the delivery. As in, the heroine drove me slightly batty. The 2nd book was better, but there was still something missing for me.<br><br>Now you're probably sitting there and thinking to yourself, why is this crazy bitch reading book 3 when she wasn't thrilled about the first 2? Well because I knew that the first two books the author was still coming into her own as a writer, but I loved where the series was heading. Possessive, slightly domineering, sexy as hell alpha male brothers?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380436821ra/883097.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Well after writing this book, I'm pretty sure the author thought<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789083.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Because everything that bothered me in the first two books was nowhere to be found here. <b>I LOVED IT.</b><br><br>I'm a sucker for a second chance romance, and this one delivered it in spades!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384193213i/6809627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Four years ago Lilly and Cash met by chance at a coffee shop. And as in true Mayson brothers fashion, that's all the time Cash needed to know that Lilly is his "one". They date and finally share an amazing night together...only for things to fall apart the very next day.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383937826i/6709420.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Cash is head over heals for Lilly, but when his crazy ex (hookup, fuck buddy?) comes back with the news that she's pregnant he has no other choice but to do the right thing and be there for his baby. So he makes the ultimate sacrifice, breaking not only his own heart but Lilly's in the process.<br><br>When Lilly receives Cash's cold text message that it's over between them, it's the last thing she expects. The fact that she is now pregnant and Cash is not at all the man she though he was is not an easy pill to swallow. But she knows what she has to do for her unborn baby, and that's stay strong and move on, raising her baby as a single mom.<br><br>Now years later when their paths cross again, can Cash win Lilly's heart once more or is the damage he did between them irreparable?<br><br>The one thing I really love about Aurora's alpha males, is when they see the woman they want they go after her with all the grace of a speeding train. Nothing gets in their way. They know what they want, and they <b>will</b> have it. Cash knows that he will stop at nothing to win Lilly back, he just needs to prove to her that he's not the man she thinks he is.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789084.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I forgive you, Cash. I definitely approve of your methods in making up for lost time.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424456ra/846150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But it wasn't all hot sexy loving. (Which I will never have too much of in these books) I absolutely loved seeing the romance grow between Lilly and Cash. Cash was this perfect combination of dirty talking alpha male and sweet.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789085.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was also the added element of Cash's psycho ex to keep things interesting. And let me tell you...Jules?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789086.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Talk about your crazy bitches. Good lord. The things that she did had me screaming at my kindle in the middle of an empty room.<br><br>You know how sometimes there are these characters that just make you want to take off your earrings, put on your ass kicking boots, take out a baseball bat, jump into your kindle and beat the ever loving hell out of them? Well, Jules was that character for me.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789087.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wish that Lilly had stood up to her, but that never really happened. Luckily Cash and his family really came through in that. <br><br>But gah! Jules!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393968731ra/8789088.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let me end this before I go off on another Jules tangent here. I adored this book. The second chance love story, the added element of their kids together, catching up with the rest of the Mason brothers, it was fantastic.<br><br>You get your scorching hot sex scenes with a great story and I for one cannot wait for Nico's book...especially after the teaser in this one.<br><br>If you liked the first two books, you will love this one. And if you're like me and the first two books weren't that great for you, then read this one and you will change your mind about the series. Aurora Rose Reynolds is definitely an auto buy author for me after this one.<br><br><br><i>***ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review*</i><br><br>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <span id="freeText16105663552386566821" style="display:none">I freaking LOVED.EVERY.SINGLE.MINUTE.OF.THIS!!!!!!!!<br><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/HumdkG0" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><br><br>So I love Asher, I even Loved Trevor, BUT I ABSOLUTELY Loved Cash, this one is my favorite so far. Aurora just continues to make me sit here dying for the next one in this series. I will be forever a Mayson Boys Fan!!!!!<br><br>We first heard a little bit about Cash and Lilly in Until Trevor and I was dying to get my hands on this one. Well let me tell you Aurora did not disappoint me at all. I LOVED every single minute of this one. When Cash and Lilly first met they fell hard for each other. Cash knew that Lilly was his one. Cash had end things after he made a life altering decision. Although he lost Lilly he gained a son Jaxson. Cash would do anything to protect his son even keep him from his useless ex who wants nothing to do with Jaxson. <br><br>Lilly although she was devastated when Cash up and left her, she had to keep going with life because she found out she was pregnant. After trying to call Cash to tell him and not being able to talk to him directly she is left on her own with her pregnancy. Ashlyn became Lilly’s life and she has done everything in her power to be a single mom and provide for her daughter. <br>“Why can’t I hate you?” Her words are quiet, and I can hardly make them out.<br><br><b>I whisper into her ear before kissing her under it, “Because I am your one, too.”</b><br><br>When Cash runs into Lilly at a playground with Jaxson he is shocked to see her with a little girl who looks exactly like his son. Cash vows then that he will do whatever he has to do to get Lilly and his daughter back into his life. <br><br><b>"I’m going to make you fall in love with me again."</b> <br><br>Lilly is someone who I will never take for granted, because I know how it feels to be without her and the light that she brings to my life.<br><br>Their road to their second chance is not an easy one for them. They are met with obstacles along the way including Cash’s crazy ex-wife. She is one woman I that if I could have reached through my kindle and bitch slapped her I would have done it in a heartbeat. <br><br><b>“I know we have a lot to work on, and I know that it’s going to take time for us to rebuild what was broken, but I also know that if we do, we will have something that is beyond anything that either of us thought possible.”</b><br><br>Lilly is afraid to open her heart again to Cash, and Cash refuses to take no for an answer from Lilly. I truly loved how Aurora brought together their second chance romance story. <br><br>The kids I ABSOLULTEY loved Ashlyn and Jaxson. Those two kids were awesome, funny, and had me laughing more than once throughout the story. <br><br>Kudos to you Aurora for not disappointing me and giving me another Awesome Mayson Boy to read about. I cannot wait for Nico’s story (hint, hint….. I’ll take it as soon as you hit end) LOL <br>Ohh Yeahhh!!! I know what I am reading tonight!!!! Half way through Trevor and I knew I wanted the next one to be Cash and Lilly !!!!!!<br><br>I NEED More Cash and Lilly NOW Please Aurora !!!!!!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1814591859" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17246005443336169133"><b> 3.75 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was better than I thought it would be. To be honest, some of the reviews I read really turned me off of this -- but I am really happy that I tried out the audiobook and gave it a shot! I actually liked it so much that I downloaded the ebook because the little bit of the audiobook I got wasn't enough! I just want to clarify in a spoiler something that is portrayed inaccurately in some reviews...<a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[The situation with the h's pregnancy...so, I read in s</span></span>
  <span id="freeText17246005443336169133" style="display:none"><b> 3.75 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was better than I thought it would be. To be honest, some of the reviews I read really turned me off of this -- but I am really happy that I tried out the audiobook and gave it a shot! I actually liked it so much that I downloaded the ebook because the little bit of the audiobook I got wasn't enough! I just want to clarify in a spoiler something that is portrayed inaccurately in some reviews...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The situation with the h's pregnancy...so, I read in some reviews that the h gets dumped so the H can go with OW to get married and have a baby while the H tells her to just get an abortion. While some of this is true, it is not what it seems! The woman that was pregnant with the H's baby was an ex fling that told him that she would abort the baby if he didn't break ties with any other woman he was with, so he did because he wanted to have a relationship with his child. At first his relationship it's the OW was kind of platonic, but it did develop into more when he got married to her -- but it was more of a thing where he was trying to do what is best for his son, not because she was the love of his life! The h found out she was pregnant after he broke things off with her, and she reached out to him and got some nasty text messages that said that she needs to "get rid of it". Later we find out that the H knew nothing of the h's pregnancy or the text messages, which has them thinking that the OW did this. Again -- not at all as simple as it has been stated. I felt like some of these reviews were really misleading!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I am usually not one to criticize so I'm not going to point fingers, but for those potential readers out there I just want you to know that it isn't as bad as it has been made out to be! I enjoyed it. I think that some of the OW drama was a little OTT, so that was the main reason for my deduction of the .25 points ;)<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lilly and Cash's story. They meet one day in a coffee shop, and Cash knows instantly that she is his "one" (or boom) and pursues her. They have a whirlwind romance, but it is cut short when Cash finds out that a woman from his past is pregnant with his child. They are separated, and when they are reunited Cash is shocked to find out that Lilly had his daughter. They work to get over past wrongs and blend their new families together as their feelings for one another had never changed. There is a good bit of ex drama, but they do get a HEA in the end.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Lilly and Cash's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed, and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. They take a while to develop feelings, but those feeling return right away when reunited.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Cash. I felt really bad for the situation he was in with his ex, and I liked him and the Dad he was to his children.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Lilly. I liked her, but I did wish that she made the H work a little harder when they are reunited (even though the H wasn't at fault).<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low. No tissues needed.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H pushes the h away in the past when he is given an ultimatum by the OW that found out she was pregnant with his child.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some good scenes, but it doesn't take away from the storyline.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mentions of condoms, birth control, and STD status. The h lost her virginity to the H, and the H says he never went without a condom before the h.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H's ex-wife causes a lot of drama.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated for years. The H marries and divorces OW, and h had no other partners. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H was married and had a child with OW, abortion (mention), and child kidnapping.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b>This had a great jump ahead epilogue with a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got the audiobook with my scribed subscription, and I ended up paying the $3.99 on Amazon for the ebook.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> I'd call this one <u>Safe with exception</u> <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~4 year (? I don't remember it stating exactly how long) separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="17246005443336169133" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/865697343" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/865697343?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2014-release">2014-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer865697343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5654127712895946005">★★★★ <b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394057031i/8802336.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Until Lilly</b> has been one of my most anticipated releases since the moment I read the first chapter/teaser of it at the back of Until Trevor, the previous book in this series. Needless to say, I had high expectations of Cash and Lilly's story and after having read their story, I can honestly say it did not disappoint.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why can’t I hate you?” Her words are quiet, and I can hardly make them out.<br/><br/>I whisper into her ear before kissing her under it, “Because I am your one, too.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5654127712895946005" style="display:none">★★★★ <b>4 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394057031i/8802336.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Until Lilly</b> has been one of my most anticipated releases since the moment I read the first chapter/teaser of it at the back of Until Trevor, the previous book in this series. Needless to say, I had high expectations of Cash and Lilly's story and after having read their story, I can honestly say it did not disappoint.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why can’t I hate you?” Her words are quiet, and I can hardly make them out.<br><br>I whisper into her ear before kissing her under it, “Because I am your one, too.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When Cash was forced to choose between the love of his life and his unborn son, he chose the latter. As heart wrenching as it was to leave Lilly behind, he did what he had to do to be a present and responsible father to his child. Now, four years later, neither Cash nor Lilly have gotten over one another. They've tried to built up a normal life and move on from their heartbreak over losing each other but when they unexpectedly run into each other, at a kid's play hall no less, those old feelings move right back to the surface.<br><br>But after all those years of heartbreak and hurt feelings, will they ever be able to go back to the way they were before? Or will old enemies, once again, interfere and prevent them from giving their love a second chance?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394189307i/8818659.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet, sexy with a (pretty huge) touch of drama and lots of endearing moments, Until Lilly was once again a successful addition to the Until-series. So far I've enjoyed every single one of the books in this series but I think this one might be my favorite. I'm a sucker for heartbreak, dramatics and second chances when it comes to books that still have a happy ending and Cash and Lilly's story was definitely one that had all those ingredients in spades. And the side characters of the adorably cute Jax and Ashlyn made the story all the more fun to read!<br><br>Still, I have very high expectations for Nico's story as well so I'll be anxiously awaiting the release of the fourth and final book in this series!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394189307i/8818660.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5654127712895946005" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_791899834" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/791899834" />
    <a title="Stephanie*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5656015-stephanie"><img alt="Stephanie*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537524761p2/5656015.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/791899834?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie*" href="/user/show/5656015-stephanie">Stephanie*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer791899834" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1125982191717823338"><b>* 4.5 Second Chance Stars *</b><br/><br/>My Lilly...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393723355i/8756848._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>My Cash...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393790032i/8763803._SY540_.jpg' width='310' height='330' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is a beautiful second chance love story. Cash fell in love with Lilly after meeting in a coffee shop. They start to build a healthy relationship until one of Cash's conquests from the past ends up pregnant. Cash feels like he needs to do right by Jules and his future son, so he cuts ties with Lilly without much of an explanation. Lilly ends up becoming pregnant after Cash had taken her virginity and tries to get a hold of him to let him know t</span>
  <span id="freeText1125982191717823338" style="display:none"><b>* 4.5 Second Chance Stars *</b><br><br>My Lilly...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393723355i/8756848._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>My Cash...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393790032i/8763803._SY540_.jpg" width="310" height="330" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a beautiful second chance love story. Cash fell in love with Lilly after meeting in a coffee shop. They start to build a healthy relationship until one of Cash's conquests from the past ends up pregnant. Cash feels like he needs to do right by Jules and his future son, so he cuts ties with Lilly without much of an explanation. Lilly ends up becoming pregnant after Cash had taken her virginity and tries to get a hold of him to let him know that she is pregnant. Some unfortunate issues and miscommunication lead to a heartbreaking end to their relationship. <br><br>I don't think I've cried so much at the beginning of a book than what I did in this story. Ugly, sobbing, mess! I felt so bad for Lilly!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380389597ra/750800.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Luckily, fate leads Cash and Lilly back together three years later and from here we get to see their relationship spark to life and build back to the inferno these two used to have in the past.<br><br>I will say that, one issue I normally have with second chance romance books, is when certain couples spend so much time trying to rebuild their trust due to their misunderstandings &amp; miscommunication in the past, that the overall story is affected by the stubbornness and lack of forgiveness by one or both of the characters. <br><br><b>This is not that type of story!</b> Loved both Lilly and Cash. They had their issues in the past, including many misunderstandings, however they were able to talk about their problems from the very beginning and forgive one another. This allows the reader to see their story unfold and it is quite beautiful.<br><br>Most of the drama, occurs with the help of Cash's other baby mama, Jules. What the hell was wrong with her anyways? I knew the bitch was crazy from Until Trevor, but I did <i>not</i> know the bitch was <i>that crazy.</i> She needs a padded cell and some medication, because she is not right in the head. She was a major participant in causing a lot of drama for both Cash and Lilly. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393724401i/8756926.jpg" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes...she did, and she is whacked out. Luckily, her drama made Cash &amp; Lilly's relationship that much stronger. I have only one thing to say to you Jules...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381121244ra/4274403.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But what I loved about this story is that no matter how difficult their lives became because of Jules, Cash and Lilly remained true to one another and their relationship never wavered. I love when couples do not succumb to the stupidity &amp; jealousy of others, &amp; in this story that was mainly, Jules.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380367242ra/719723.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was truly sad to see their story end because I <i>loved it that much!</i> The epilogue was also a fabulous addition to their story! I loved that it was actually <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[13 years later, so we get to see both Ashlyn &amp; Jax as teenagers <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. So good &amp; funny I might add!!<br><br>Seriously though, I love this author! Aurora, you are freaking awesome!! I love the whole Until series, and <i>cannot</i> wait for Sophie &amp; Nico's story!! You know how to write a great male character! Bring on more of the Mayson men!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393788564ra/8763506.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>EARLY RELEASE!!!! Only $3.99 on Amazon!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393678539ra/8751098.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/402443.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br>COVER LUST!!! Holy moley! :)<br><br>OMG that teaser, holy shit!!! I need this book RIGHT. FUCKING. NOW.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1125982191717823338" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/963326258?book_show_action=true">Jun 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer12735264410169218836"><br/><b>***4 I ♥ Cash Mayson Stars***</b><br/><br/>Hands down my favorite of the series so far. <br/><br/>This one felt more realistic, had more feeling and was a more well-rounded story. <br/><br/>Years ago, Lilly and Cash's lives intersected.<br/><br/>My darling Cash...he had to make a horrible decision. Neither would give him 100% what he wanted, but he had to do what he felt was right.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045372.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Lilly was left with a big ol' slice of "Life's Not Fair" pie. She picked herself up and did the best she could with the cards she was abruptly dealt. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045373.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>By accide</span>
  <span id="freeText12735264410169218836" style="display:none"><br><b>***4 I ♥ Cash Mayson Stars***</b><br><br>Hands down my favorite of the series so far. <br><br>This one felt more realistic, had more feeling and was a more well-rounded story. <br><br>Years ago, Lilly and Cash's lives intersected.<br><br>My darling Cash...he had to make a horrible decision. Neither would give him 100% what he wanted, but he had to do what he felt was right.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045372.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lilly was left with a big ol' slice of "Life's Not Fair" pie. She picked herself up and did the best she could with the cards she was abruptly dealt. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045373.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By accident, their paths cross again....life is a bit different now for both Cash and Lilly. Can true love be given a second chance? Can they have the life that was taken away from them by Cash's vindictive, baby mama Jules?<br><br>Can I just say that Jules was quite the piece of crazy work! That woman was full of so much ugly, bitter jealousy. She didn't care who she hurt, who she stepped on or who was around to hear her selfish and vile words.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045374.gif" width="500" height="232" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I tried to sympathize with Cash on why he kept trying with her...but I would have given up long ago. The only thing that crazy bitch would be getting from me would be <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045375.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>ESPECIALLY her last fucking stunt! I mean seriously?!?! I'm pretty sure if I could have reached into my Kindle, I would have ripped that bitch apart! <br><br>I think my favorite thing about this book is that the situation that ripped Cash and Lilly apart years ago wasn't a lingering factor. ARR could have decided to draw this drama out for pages on end, making Cash grovel for forgiveness or have Lilly not believe Cash about his knowledge of what happened with her....but she didn't. Outside factors were constantly throwing wrenches in their lives, but not once did you doubt the love. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Lilly, your kind of sweet is hard to come by, so when you get even just a little taste of it, you want more. I'm saying that as a man who knows."</b>
</blockquote> <br><br>Overall, this book was a story about family, love and second chances. Two people who were given a second chance to have the life they should have started years ago. <br><br>But don't you worry......mixed right in there with all this mushy awesomeness is the Mayson sex drive you come to know and love. I'd take a Cash Mayson punishment any time. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135476ra/10045376.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And there you have it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403135881ra/10045407.gif" width="260" height="260" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1361363448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2492555193377678933">Either a whole bunch of my GR friends are crazy, or I'm the most hard-to-please bitch in existence and I should just give up reading contemporary romances. Something is definitely up, and it ain't me, beyotches! <br/><br/>Now I'm assuming you should read Lily in series order, which would make this book 3. I didn't, not sure if that makes any difference, so I'm just going to tell it as I see it for <i>this</i> story<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[The story opens with Cash meeting Lilly, wooing her and taking her virginity. Then f</span></span>
  <span id="freeText2492555193377678933" style="display:none">Either a whole bunch of my GR friends are crazy, or I'm the most hard-to-please bitch in existence and I should just give up reading contemporary romances. Something is definitely up, and it ain't me, beyotches! <br /><br />Now I'm assuming you should read Lily in series order, which would make this book 3. I didn't, not sure if that makes any difference, so I'm just going to tell it as I see it for <i>this</i> story<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The story opens with Cash meeting Lilly, wooing her and taking her virginity. Then finding out another woman he used to sleep with is pregnant, he swiftly (the next day) proceeds to dump Lily <i>over the phone</i> like a premier league arsehole. With me so far? Is there, <i>any way</i> that a self-respecting woman would not want to string this man up by his balls for such behaviour? Yes? Maybe? What about if you then find <i>yourself</i> pregnant? You'd be pissed right? Sure, you'd cry and mourn and gnash your teeth and rend your garments at the vagaries of fate but, you'd get your hands on a double barrel shot gun too, right? No? You'd still be reasonable? Think, "We're over but the right thing is to tell this dirtbag who fucked me, impregnated me and dumped me that he's going to be a father." Fantastic! Move over Mother Teresa, there's a new girl in town. So, what would it take? What? To get really, really steaming, murderously, mad? Errm? How about a text response to your request to talk that you 'take care' of the problem as he's already having a baby with his 'soon-to-be wife'. Now? Please? Please can I shoot the motherfucker <i>now</i>?! Yes! Well, no, because Lily didn't follow the 53rd golden rule of dating; never sleep with a man if you don't know where he lives. So, no buckshot in this buck's buttocks, Lily.<br /><br />Three years later Lily, having scuttled off back to Alaska to lick her wounds and birth her baby, is back in the exact same town as Cash, because after all, she had such a great experience the last time she was in that state; yep clear from Alaska to Tennessee for a new job, because there was <i>nowhere</i> else in the whole landmass that is the USA, <i>between</i> these two geographical points, that Lily could have possibly found gainful employment. And boyo having now dumps the gal he married and having gotten sole custody of his son, takes one look at Lily and says .....<br /><br />“I want it back.” <br /><br />Now you will hear tales of Lily being Cash's One and that the Mayson boys have some kind of magical dicks that hones in on their soul mates and once they've locked and loaded on said target they don't let go and that it's all written in the stars, yada, yada, yada.....I don't know anything about that, as this is my first encounter with this family, but, it's all bullshit, or, at least it's bullshit in <i>this</i> author's hands, because all this story did was pissed me the hell off. Why? Because regardless of what was going on in Cash's mind, Lily's reaction to this whole debacle was so out and out <i>implausible</i> it renders everything, <i>every</i> thing else a total waste of time, a mote point. There was no drama leading up to a reunion; Cash slid back in smooth as Slick Rick, Lilly barely raises her voice, she was too busy wondering how soon she could hump his leg that she tucked her supposed heartbreak, her anger and her pride into the front of Cash's pants with a 'Oh well, I guess it was just a misunderstanding and now we are back together.' Seriously?? For Christ sake woman, even if not for yourself, whallop him one for the 3 years your daughter went without a father! Jesus * shakes head* This bitch be crazy. And I wish that I could state that that was were the crazy-train terminated. But nope, because this type of author is never happy unless they lay on crazy with a shovel.<br /><br />We also have to contend with the crazy ex, though I have yet to comprehend the reason for her derangement (maybe it was explained in the first 2 books?) Lilly loses her job based on some wackjob acting by ex and doesn't have a chance to explain to her boss? That's unrealistic and....stupid. Then Lilly apparently goes to jail for a week over some weird plot regarding fraud? It's all just...also stupid and makes absolutely no sense. There were all sorts of plot strings that were never fully picked-up, i.e. who the hell was David? Why was he introduced? Was there a point? Why was Cash's family cold to Lily if he'd initially explained (before the fucking and the leaving) she was his One, didn't they all know of the Mayson Magical Dick Radar? How could it be wrong? But the wowza of all crazy, is the ending. Lets just for a second go with the premise that this small-town, southern, crazy ex was so unhinged that she would mastermind the kidnapping of a child, lets further pretend that she was also under surveillance (no indication of that in the story but, what-the-hell...*shrug* Who cares about plot development ) so that by the time it was all said and done the police were at the right place, at the right time; can we really go still further and suspend all thoughts of reality to believing that a THREE year old could be the real hero of the piece? Run across fields, find a house, get a call put through? <i>Three year old</i>? No. Reynolds just helps us all and give it up already <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Let's just be honest, this whole novel is unbelievably weak, in my opinion, the dialogue is abysmal, plot development nonexistent. and any sniff of dramatic tension is extinguished by waves of implausibility. I really didn't like it, but even if everything else was passable, Lily's lack of backbone would have had me giving this 1star regardless. This could have been a great set up of a jilted woman being left to raise a kid alone, but only a few pages gets spent on this and spent really badly. Instead we see them reconcile without a single raised word. Good for them. Not so fun for the me, the reader.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer318493707992185957"><i>
  <b>4 Cash Lovin' Stars!</b>
</i> This book was worth the wait!<br/><br/><a href='http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/excited_zpsca072db4.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

Swoonworthy Cash with his all consuming sexy talk had me saying "Trevor who?" in no time. <br/><br/>Cash knew instantly that Lilly was his true love but circumstances beyond his control arose and he had to make a tough decision. He broke Lilly's heart and stopped all contact</span>
  <span id="freeText318493707992185957" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>4 Cash Lovin' Stars!</b>
</i> This book was worth the wait!<br><br><a href="http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/excited_zpsca072db4.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392101540ra/8500739.gif" alt=" photo excited_zpsca072db4.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh how I love these Mayson brothers! I'm so fickle with my love for them. First I loved Asher. Then Trevor came along and it was instant lust which means I had to let Asher go. Swoonworthy Cash with his all consuming sexy talk had me saying "Trevor who?" in no time. <br><br>Cash knew instantly that Lilly was his true love but circumstances beyond his control arose and he had to make a tough decision. He broke Lilly's heart and stopped all contact. Four years later many things have changed when their paths cross. This time Cash was determined to not let her get away. <br><br><a href="http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/brulianicon4_zpse20ecb23.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393709332i/8755123.png" alt=" photo brulianicon4_zpse20ecb23.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cash and Lilly's story had a really romantic feel to it. I loved that a lot of story was devoted to just Cash and Lilly recapturing their love for each other and making up for lost time. Their chemistry was amazing! <br><br>Jax and Ashlyn completely melted my heart. <br><br><a href="http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/girlandboyholdinghands_zps56e9088b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393711848i/8755542.jpg" alt=" photo girlandboyholdinghands_zps56e9088b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was such treat to have two adorable children play a big part in this story. They helped create a beautiful family unit.<br><br>Of course there is a crazy ex-wife trying her best to create all sorts of drama and chaos. I admit I wished Lilly would have had the opportunity to give Jules a good beat down a few times. <br><br>It's always a delight to have the rest of the Mayson family involved in the storyline. They are such a fun group who love each other and have each other's back. <br><br>My only <i>small</i> nitpicking issue was the grammatical errors in places.<br><br><br>Side note: Aurora Reynolds you are such a tease! Giving a sneak peak into Nico's story makes me think this delicious badboy is going to melt my heart. <br><br><b>BRING IT ON!</b><br><br> <a href="http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/po_zpsb4d6ee70.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392917817ra/8633092.gif" alt=" photo po_zpsb4d6ee70.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>_______________________________________________<br><br>Is it March 5th yet?<br><br><a href="http://s838.photobucket.com/user/lisajensn/media/bartletheadsmackgif_zpsa806f279.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389633258ra/8044638.gif" alt=" photo bartletheadsmackgif_zpsa806f279.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="318493707992185957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5274596463756691960"><b>5 Second Chance Stars!</b> <br/><br/>Four years ago Cash made the hardest decision of his life: give up on the love of his life in order to protect the life of his unborn child.   <span id="freeText5274596463756691960" style="display:none"><b>5 Second Chance Stars!</b> <br><br>Four years ago Cash made the hardest decision of his life: give up on the love of his life in order to protect the life of his unborn child. He unwisely hooked up with an evil bitch and she forced him to be with her in order to keep the pregancy. He chooses his unborn child but losing Lilly means losing a part of himself along with it.<br>Now, divorced from his crazy ex-wife and with full custody of Jax, he coincidently runs into Lily again, only to find out that when he left Lilly, he also left a daughter behind.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399484410i/9558040._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This time Cash is not willing to let the love of his life go away... Or his kids for that matter. He wants he's family and he's decided to do everything in his power to keep it. <br>But when their pasts and the secrets and lies that kept them apart are brought back, how will Cash win this fight? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> A beautiful and emotional love story about redemption and second chances. One of the most heartwarming stories I've read lately. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, dual POV. Addictive and absolutely engaging. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> I loved Cash!! Probably my favorite Mayson brother so far. He goes after what he wants, isn't afraid to fight or apologize and like the others is the perfect alpha male. Lilly was also amazing, I loved how forgiving she was and the golden heart she has. She was amazing with both kids and Cash. Jax and Ashlyn were the cutest little things. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot.<br> <b>HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. Books 2 and this book started off on the wrong foot for me. I know why Cash dumped Lilly in the beginning but it just sat wrong with me.   <span id="freeText18128550037205539933" style="display:none">I kind of wish I had read the first book after reading book 2 and 3. Asher's (1st Book) book was perfection. Books 2 and this book started off on the wrong foot for me. I know why Cash dumped Lilly in the beginning but it just sat wrong with me. I'm a single mom and I know what it's like to have no help raising a child, so it not something that I can easily dismiss. Especially for the reason she got left on her own. If I take that out of the equation, I did like these two when they finally get back together. BUT...then his ex caused so many problems with Lilly and they were serious problems. I just felt like she got screwed. I need another <i>Asher</i> book and I hope Nico's will provide that.</span>

He built a life with the bitch and their son and tried to make the marriage work.<br />Even after the divorce he never sought out Zeroine. It was by chance that they met again and Zeroine did not need persuasion to accept Zero back. As a friendly reviewer says, this Zeroine is a waste of hair spray. Without a backbone and a look from Zero is enough for her to lose her panties and spread her legs for him. The icing on the cake is that she got celibate taking care of their daughter, while he played house and had sex with the bitch. <br />Minus 1 star.<br /><br /><b>==&gt;Re-read in May 10, 2016</b><br /><br />2 ⭐⭐ - Meh!<br /><br /><b>==&gt;Read in March 02, 2014</b><br /><br />A heroína aceita tudo muito facilmente e o herói ainda fica com ciúmes de supostos relacionamentos que ela possa ter tido... E ele que casou e tentou fazer o casamento dar certo? A heroína é muito passiva e sem personalidade... basta uns beijinhos que ela já baixa as calcinhas...<br />------------<br />The heroine accepts all too easily, and the hero is still jealous of alleged relationships that she may have had. <br />And he married a bitch and still tried to make the marriage work? WTF!<br />The heroine is too passive and without personality ... just some kissing that she's dropping the panties...</span>

<div id="review_762832327" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762832327" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762832327?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762832327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13912686379675822866"><b>5 second chance stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393833113i/8770401._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>When we got a glimpse into how Lilly & Cash’s story was going to unfold in Until Trevor, I knew that this was going to be a flippin’ fantastic story and a great addition to one of my favorite series. <br/><br/>In one moment Cash knew he had met the one, in three short months he knew he would love her until he took his last breath. But it isn’t until four years later that he gets his second chance to win back what he was forced to lose.<br/><br/>When the Lilly meets Cash, the last thing she wa</span>
  <span id="freeText13912686379675822866" style="display:none"><b>5 second chance stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393833113i/8770401._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When we got a glimpse into how Lilly &amp; Cash’s story was going to unfold in Until Trevor, I knew that this was going to be a flippin’ fantastic story and a great addition to one of my favorite series. <br><br>In one moment Cash knew he had met the one, in three short months he knew he would love her until he took his last breath. But it isn’t until four years later that he gets his second chance to win back what he was forced to lose.<br><br>When the Lilly meets Cash, the last thing she wants to be is another woman that he simply beds and moves on from. Falling in love with him was one of the easiest things she had ever done, falling out of love with him would soon prove to be impossible.<br><br>When the she-bitch makes him chose between his child and Lilly, he makes the only choice he can. He picks his son, Jax, but that marriage made in hell didn’t last long and Cash finally got his son and his freedom. Now four years later when he sees her again, it’s not just Lilly that he sees. A little girl that is standing at her side, a little girl he never knew he had, Ashlyn.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393833113i/8770402._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>He let her slip through his fingers once and now that he has his second chance at love with the only girl he’s ever loved there is no way he is going to let her go. <br><br>Together, Lilly and Cash navigate falling in love again, raising their children and having to deal with the ex that just won’t go away. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393833114i/8770403.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I have absolutely loved every single one of the Mayson boys, each one gives you just something so different but they each share similar traits. I loved that Cash knew he could push but that he had to not be too forceful, there was pain that lingered between them and Cash was patient when needed. <br><br>The way Cash was with his kids was so touching, so many moments where his heart just swelled from what he finally had, what he nearly lost... it was just utterly beautiful. Lilly was such a perfect heroine! She had so many reasons to act out given the way their relationship had ended, raising her daughter alone for the last four years and thinking that Cash knew all along and didn’t want them. But she was not, she loved him and even though she wanted to protect her heart, she never tried to keep him out. <br><br>Aurora Rose Reynolds has created this stunning cast of hot, over the top alpha males that are completely lovable. We get a peek at Nico’s <b>boom</b> moment and it gives us a great lead into his book.<br><br>I loved that the epilogue gives us a glimpse into their lives not just a few months down the road but years later. Getting to see this interaction with them roughly twelve years into the future was so enjoyable. <br><br>If you have not checked out this series yet, you really should add it to your list; each story gives you a bit of drama that allows the men’s possessive streaks to come out, they are all over the top alpha males that know what they want the minute they find the one and their eyes do not wander. Man-whores that just need to find the one that makes them want to settle down. Now the wait for Nico &amp; Sophie begins!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13912686379675822866" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16643464282840458366">** 12/15/16 audio reread. ...again. in anticipation of the Until Ashlyn release ...**<br/><br/>another Audio "reread"!! <br/><br/>I loved this story. I originally read this well over a year ago, before I got pickier with my books. <br/><br/>Cash met Lily and fell head over heels. He knew she was his "boom" and he wanted to start a life with her. Things were going great until a woman from his past tells him she's pregnant. She tells him that he either cuts off all ties with others or she will terminate the pregnancy. Cash has</span>
  <span id="freeText16643464282840458366" style="display:none">** 12/15/16 audio reread. ...again. in anticipation of the Until Ashlyn release ...**<br /><br />another Audio "reread"!! <br /><br />I loved this story. I originally read this well over a year ago, before I got pickier with my books. <br /><br />Cash met Lily and fell head over heels. He knew she was his "boom" and he wanted to start a life with her. Things were going great until a woman from his past tells him she's pregnant. She tells him that he either cuts off all ties with others or she will terminate the pregnancy. Cash has no choice and for the sake of his unborn child he has to break it off with Lily. He was devastated but did what he thought was best at the time, not knowing that Lily had life changing news too. <br /><br />Lily was devastated by Cash's abrupt ending of their relationship. Especially after she found out she is pregnant. She texts him and the answer she gets back breaks her heart (even though we all know it wasn't him) She goes on with her life crushed because she loved him. <br /><br />Fast forward 4 years. Lily runs into Cash with his son. He is angry at first because he thinks she has kept his daughter from him. Lily let's him have it. He has no idea what she is talking about. Cash heart has been broken over losing lily before and he knows that he was never letting her or their child out of his sight.<br /><br /> I was heartbroken when Cash broke it off with Lily even though I understood why. I did not like that he attempted to make his marriage work with the ex wife because he didn't love her and she was holding their son over his head. I also felt he could have been more apologetic for all that Lily went through. He did go above and beyond once they were back together. He was alpha-licious and took charge of the relationship. He would NOT lose the love of his life a second time. <br /><br />Jules, the mother of his son, was a psycho bitch and made their lives hell.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16643464282840458366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=4-or-more-stars">4-or-more-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=arc-reviewed">arc-reviewed</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6294320-carol-starangel-s-reviews-allen?shelf=blog-tour">blog-tour</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer839650431" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2535882010540340798"><strong>Book</strong> – Until Lilly (Until #3)<br/><strong>Author</strong> – Aurora Rose Reynolds<br/><strong>Publication Date</strong> – February 28, 2014<br/><strong>Type</strong> – No Cliffhanger Series<br/><strong>Genre</strong> – Romance, New Adult<br/><strong>Rating</strong> – 4 out of 5 Stars<br/><br/><em>Book kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review.</em><br/><br/><strong>Review</strong><br/>I loved it!! I loved the premise of the story and the journey Ms. Reynolds took me on.  I can’t say whether this is my favorite in the series or not….I am bass ackwards and started from the end….but now that I read this book…I’m definitely going back and re</span>
  <span id="freeText2535882010540340798" style="display:none"><strong>Book</strong> – Until Lilly (Until #3)<br><strong>Author</strong> – Aurora Rose Reynolds<br><strong>Publication Date</strong> – February 28, 2014<br><strong>Type</strong> – No Cliffhanger Series<br><strong>Genre</strong> – Romance, New Adult<br><strong>Rating</strong> – 4 out of 5 Stars<br><br><em>Book kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review.</em><br><br><strong>Review</strong><br>I loved it!! I loved the premise of the story and the journey Ms. Reynolds took me on.  I can’t say whether this is my favorite in the series or not….I am bass ackwards and started from the end….but now that I read this book…I’m definitely going back and reading about Cash’s brothers!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395014674i/8935742.jpg" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ms. Reynolds had the ability to transport me into the story and follow along with Lilly and Cash….I felt Lilly’s pain with that text message she received…hence my FU updates towards Cash….I held my breath when Cash and Lilly set eyes on each other at the play gym for the kids….<br><br>Why only 4 stars instead of 5?  I guess it had to do with Jules and Cash ---- if Cash knew what Jules was capable of then why didn’t he protect Lilly and the kids better.  It broke my heart that Jax had to go through that pain of having a womb donor who only used him to manipulate Cash.  I also had a problem with the reason why Jules did something at the end of the story….it was a bit of a shocker.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395014674i/8935743._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In no way shape or form did I subtract stars for the writing ability of Ms. Reynolds…I’m telling you that woman can write – she can write a scene and it smoothly and effortlessly plays in front of your eyes!  I empathized with Lilly – I fell in love with Lilly and the strong heroine she portrayed in this story.  She was truly my hero!<br><br><strong>Re-Cap</strong><br>Cash and Lilly have a brief encounter and relationship but they fall hard and fall fast.  But does every rainbow have a pot of gold at the end?  HELL NO….and just like a rainbow….real life comes crashing down on Cash and he must make a decision – to him he makes the best choice and ends up breaking Lilly’s heart and leaving her a single mother.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395014674i/8935744.png" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Years later, a chance meeting throws Cash and Lilly together and lo’ and behold – their little children look exactly like twins.  Cash thinks that Lilly kept his daughter a secret while Lilly has nothing but hatred toward Cash for abandoning her while pregnant.<br><br>Once Cash and Lilly find out the truth….Cash is determined to get the love of his life back – well the best he can with his annoying and bitch of an ex sticking her skanky ass in where it doesn’t belong.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395014674i/8935745._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>Wrap-Up</strong><br>Once reading this book, I have found a new author to go all “fan-girling” over….I have to go back and read her other books now!!<br><br><strong>For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394342368i/8839977._SX540_.jpg" width="”400”" alt=" photo banner_zps637f7ed8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
